< review>
Smokin Barrel is a first class facility. The facility is very clean and maintained to highest standards. I ventured into another range in Burbank and the targets kept swinging back and forth inches in each direction due to air flow it was difficult to enjoy the range. The Smokin Barrel has the most modern systems available. I never smell fumes and I can pickup my brass no questions asked. So best for last. With an influx of new gun owners safety is my biggest concern. The entire staff is the most professional, helpful and easy going folks I have met. The range masters are on top of it always providing a safe range and helping those who need help. Nobody ever gets yelled at or embarrassed. It's the perfect place for the novice or expert to plink and have fun. See you there and don't forget to tip the range masters and or staff although not expected ever. They are what makes this place so unique. Thank you Smokin Barrel.<//review>

< text>
I love this town and beach!  We are locals, lived here in SLO County from birth. We have always wanted to camp by the ocean in Avila but have never been able to get in. We have managed to stay at the RV camping up on the bluff. So, I was so excited when I managed to get a site at the Nobi area! Campsite #5 was the only site I could find available. For 4 nights!  Not over the weekend, but we were super happy to get one at all. The day we were leaving to come camp I checked the website and found out that Nobi 3 was available for two of the 4 nights we were there!  If you‚Äôve been to Nobi, you know that site 5 is directly behind 3 and a camper in 3 can pretty much totally block site 5‚Äôs view of the ocean. Well, it was too late to cancel our original reservation without full penalty. But to us, it was worth it to pay for both sites to be able to have the unobstructed view of the ocean for two of the days.  I quickly reserved #3 and we were on our way. We stayed the first night with a small motor home between us and the ocean. The second night, the view was ours and we enjoyed it immensely. On the 3rd day the camp host texted me and asked when we were coming in. I responded that we were there already, parked in space 5. A few minutes later the camp hosts drove up, we had an issue and that we could not occupy 2 spaces unless we had another camper in the other one. We explained what happened. Their only response was, see the port for reimbursement.  We‚Äôll we didn‚Äôt mind losing the money, especially if we had unknowingly broken the rules. The next day a huge Tiffan motor home with a full size Jeep pulled in, right in front of us. Gone was all of our view.  We were so disappointed. If we‚Äôd known the hosts were going to cancel one of reservations for that day, we would have chooses to move into the view site. But we had been told nothing about opening one of the sites we paid for to another camper.  My husband went to talk to the office the next day. They basically said, tough, you broke the rule, it‚Äôs too popular here for someone to have two sites and not occupy both. No refund. We ended up enjoying some days and hours with the spot in front of us empty. But the whole experience with the hosts was so negative it took a lot of joy out of our vacation. It could have been handled so much better, we are generally rule followers and would have cooperated with the rules, we just would have liked to have more friendly understanding conversations with the representatives of the port.<//text>

< review>
Some of the best views for camping. It's within walking distance to the Port & services. They have showers and laundry services for quarters. The downside is it's all first come first serve with no reservations. It fills up fast so come before the weekend and holidays or you might not get a spot. It also pretty experience for camping and a 14 day max< /review>

Caliber Collision European Auto Body offers the absolute finest level of service and repair. On our way home from the accident, we stopped for an assessment at a Caliber location near our home. Service Advisor Evan Murray was knowledgeable and accommodating. To make our experience easier, were able to leave our vehicle there and it was transported by flatbed tow truck to their European repair facility. Our Service Advisor, Lance Leonard, was with us every step along the way and kept us fully informed on the progress of our restoration. We appreciate his professionalism and personal attention to detail. General Manager Karen Michel even helped us with a vehicle issue that could only be remedied while the bumper was off our car. I only asked if I could make the minor unrelated repair for myself, and she generously asked her technicians to make the correction for us. Jessica in the front office was a pleasure to work with as well. Most importantly, our car looks better than before the incident ever occurred. Caliber Collision European Auto Body is in a class of its own!

James and Tina Goodjohn

Okay, THIS is the plumbing company I will use from now on. Forever.

Like you, I was also searching online for reputable plumbers in SD. Let me help you out right now -- your search is over! Don't waste another minute of your time; just call APG and rest assured you've made the right choice.

I called APG today for a slow drain in my kitchen sink. From the moment Ryan answered the phone (on the first ring), my experience with APG was fabulous. Ryan was helpful, competent, and friendly, letting me know they could come out this afternoon. I received texts throughout the morning, updating me on my estimated appt timeframe (within 30 minutes, mind you, not the "we'll be there between 8am and 8pm" stuff), and also a text letting me know when they were on the way to my place.

Garrett, the service manager, showed up right on time. He was extremely professional, friendly, careful, and informative. With some initial examination and troubleshooting, he was able to get the drain moving faster. But he did advise me that, unfortunately, the problem wouldn't be completely resolved as there was likely a larger underlying issue with a broken or fractured pipe inside the wall. As such, he wrote up detailed notes on recommendations for moving forward for me to pass along to my landlord. When I asked him how much for the service call, he said zero -- since he wasn't able to fully eliminate the problem, there was no charge. Every other place I've ever worked with charges a flat fee just for the service call. Incredible!

It's obvious to me that APG operates on straightforward, honest, and ethical business practices and that their reputation is very important to them. I would give them the highest recommendation for customer service, quality, and competency.</text>

We did Confinement and The Gift last night and it was an amazing experience! For a group of 4, both rooms were very doable and action-packed. We recommend both!

Confinement was our favorite. It provided a thrilling plot that had unique puzzles that were appropriately difficult and thought provoking. There were 1-2 times where we were stumped and needed a nudge in the right direction, but the puzzles were very outside the box and creative.

The Gift was very visually exciting! It was very clear that there was a lot of effort placed into the room organization and decor. The puzzles were a lot more linear and rewarding. The puzzle-solving felt a bit more classic than Confinement‚Äôs, so it was easier to follow through the story and know what to do next.

Our hosts, Sarah and Zach, were very good game masters that immersed us into the stories and enthusiastically guided us throughout our journey. Their clues provided just enough help to nudge us in the right direction without removing our ability to be able to solve it ourselves. We will definitely be asking for them when we return for the other rooms!<//Review>

< Review>
Had my first escape room experience at Red Door and it was so immersive and fun! Our game master Aleks was extremely charismatic, answered all of our questions before starting and was very attentive while we were in the escape room as well. Even when we weren't asking for hints the encouragement and playful questions they asked us via the screen in the room assisted both with morale and getting us to think outside the box for solutions. I would love to have them as a gm again! We played through the Once Upon a Time scenario and the attention to details in the room/decor help you get into the whole thing that much more. The puzzles were challenging, but definitely doable with a group and the hints that Aleks gave us. I don't want to give too much away, but if you love fairy tales or high fantasy this is the room for you. Figuring each part out felt rewarding as the puzzles take thought and effort. Also, even outside of the escape room is decorated so beautifully- where we were briefed/locker area was like being in a sand castle!!! Definitely want to try other rooms they have and will see if I can request Aleks as our game master again!< /Review>
